High Note Humor is a South Jersey / Philadelphia comedy group. Founded by Kevin Hurley and James Cristiano, our goal is to provide an outlet for the area&#039;s best comedians while producing great material. Some of our previous venues include Filomena&#039;s Restaurant, Camden County College, Nippers Pub, and Philadelphia&#039;s High Note Cafe among others. 

Current members of High Note Humor include:

KEVIN HURLEY
Kevin is an active comedian in the tristate area and also a member of Actor&#039;s Equity Association. He was a Philly&#039;s Phunniest finalist this past year and recently won the Sarcasm Comedy Competition. 

JAMES CRISTIANO
James currently produces shows with High Note Humor and writes comedy in his free time. James is pursuing a degree in Entertainment Management at Drexel University and recently spent the summer in New York City working as a web manager for urban comedy website theruckus.com and as an assistant to comedians JB Smoove and Lynne Koplitz. In 2008, James was honored with the prestigious award for most handsome and charming man in Philadelphia (by his mother) but lost it in 2009 to Kevin Hurley. 

STEVEN BRYAN
Steven is black.

NEILL CARROLL
A native of Cherry Hill, New Jersey, Neill has been active in show business since the age of 17, when he first interned on the set of the feature film &quot;The Doghouse&quot; and appeared on WIP&#039;s Morning Show with Angelo Cataldi.  He earned his Bachelor&#039;s Degree in Film and Media Arts from Temple University in 2007 and began performing comedy shortly thereafter.  His screenplay, &quot;Pro Cons&quot;, won &quot;Best Use of Character&quot; at the 2009 Philadelphia 48 Hour Film Project, and he recently finished second place in the Philadelphia Comedy Academy&#039;s semi-annual competition.  Sadly, he has yet to receive any awards from James Cristiano&#039;s mother.
